| session_CHK | CHK-RA-VISCOUS-DC-002 DONE 2026-05-02 — User 指示「問題の原因を物理学・数学の理論に基づいて仮説考案し推理」「因子化キャッシュは悪手」「疎行列パターン固定化はまずトライ」「matrix-free low solve の精度懸念」「共通 scalar Helmholtz 近似は理論確立から」対応。N=128/T=1/alpha=4 fully-periodic static droplet validation completed on remote GPU with implicit-BDF2 viscous `defect_correction`: 810 steps to `t=1.0`, wall time 28m04s, final/max KE `3.2082084486958047e-06`, volume drift `0.0`, deformation `0.0`. RCA: this YAML is static-grid, not per-step grid rebuild (`_rebuild_freq=0`); low-order Helmholtz micro-timing on the same fitted N=128 grid gave sparse-matrix build `0.253+0.247s`, sparse LU `0.0868+0.0876s`, and one two-component triangular solve `0.146s`, so current DC low path costs roughly `1.26s/step` from Python/host assembly, two component LU factors, and repeated low solves. Root cause identified as mathematical-design mismatch: structured tensor-grid Helmholtz correction is implemented as fresh general sparse host-built problem each step. Rejected: grid rebuild as current-run cause, LU as sole bottleneck, matrix-free inaccuracy as theorem, common scalar low operator impossibility. Supported: fixed row/column sparse pattern with GPU-side value update, GPU-resident RHS/correction, and theory-first scalar Helmholtz low operator (`c=3/2` spectrally equivalent to component stress weights) as next design directions. Artifact: `docs/memo/CHK-RA-VISCOUS-DC-002_low_helmholtz_rca.md`. Source commit: `180937a9`. Main merge not performed. [SOLID-X] investigation/docs only; high-residual DC contract preserved; no production code deleted. |
| session_CHK | CHK-RA-VISCOUS-DC-001 DONE 2026-05-02 — User 指示「ResearchArchitect」「implicit BDF2 粘性項を GMRES ではなく DC で解く理論構築・実装設計・検証」「GMRES は fallback ではなく YAML 選択制」対応。New worktree `.claude/worktrees/ra-viscous-dc-20260502` / branch `ra-viscous-dc-20260502` from `main`; lock `docs/locks/ra-viscous-dc-20260502.lock.json` acquired. Theory: the BDF2 time integrator is unchanged; each step solves the high-order viscous Helmholtz equation `A_H u^*=b` by residual defect correction with low-order `A_L`, preserving the high-order fixed point and hence BDF2/space accuracy when `rho(I-omega A_L^{-1}A_H)<1`. Unlike PPE, the admissible low problem is not a constant-density Poisson solve; it is a low-order viscous Helmholtz operator sharing `mu`, `rho`, boundary topology, and periodic quotient constraints, while cross-derivative/high CCD terms remain in the high residual. Implementation: added factor-reused low-order viscous Helmholtz DC solver; implicit-BDF2 viscosity now selects `defect_correction` or `gmres` explicitly via `viscosity.solver.kind` in YAML, with DC as default and GMRES retained only as explicit comparison/diagnostic path; propagated solver tolerances/restart/DC correction controls through RunCfg/runtime/build contexts; canonical ch14/ch13 YAMLs now declare the DC solver. Validation: local `py_compile` PASS; local targeted pytest PASS for GMRES YAML selection, GMRES zero-operator, DC zero-operator, DC residual reduction, and ch14 stack config; remote `make test` PASS for `implicit_bdf2_viscosity_solver_selects_gmres`, `implicit_bdf2_viscous`, `ch14_capillary_yaml_uses_true_low_order_defect_base`, and `test_construction_uniform`; `git diff --check` PASS; paper `latexmk -xelatex -interaction=nonstopmode -halt-on-error main.tex` PASS (`paper/main.pdf`, 241 pp; existing underfull/float diagnostics only). Source commits: `39b4e386`, `0d89f976`, `9ef67ee4`. Main merge not performed. [SOLID-X] new responsibility isolated in `simulation.viscous_helmholtz_dc`; predictor selects injected solver mode rather than fallback branching; config parsing, runtime state, and numerical solve remain separated; no tested code deleted. |

| session_CHK | CHK-RA-GRID-IFACE-005 DONE 2026-05-01 — User 指示「問題の原因を物理学・数学の理論に基づいて仮説考案し推理」「今回の修正を、理論化・定式化して論文に反映して」対応。Theory/hypotheses: mixed x-periodic/y-wall capillary-wave state belongs to periodic quotient space `Q_P` and any reinitializer must be an endomorphism of `Q_P` and commute with half-period translation/reflection when IC/grid/walls do; FMM/Eikonal redistancing must impose Dirichlet seeds only on the actual zero set and physical wall-contact constraints. Validation of hypotheses: disabling reinit preserved seam but blew up at `t=7.784`, rejecting “reinit is merely harmful”; isolated RidgeEikonal on a perfectly half-period-symmetric mode-2 input produced `psi_half=3.27e-02` in one call, identifying reinit as symmetry-breaking operator; decomposed diagnostics showed FMM without ridge seeds preserved half symmetry, while ridge mask generated non-equivariant artificial zero seeds; wall-contact mass-correction also treated periodic x-image planes as walls. Fix: default RidgeEikonal no longer promotes Gaussian ridge-mask nodes to zero Dirichlet seeds; optional legacy `ridge_zero_seeds` flag retained off by default; wall-contact protected band is restricted to actual wall axes. Tests: local `test_ridge_eikonal_preserves_mixed_periodic_half_period_symmetry` and wall-contact regression PASS; remote same test PASS; existing mixed periodic velocity/FCCD scalar tests PASS. Experiments: `_tmp_ch14_capillary_n32_t8` PASS to `T=8.0`; seam gaps all `0.0`; final/max `psi_half=1.446e-04`, `p_half=3.881e-03`, `u_half=1.995e-05`, `v_half=5.003e-05`, `KE_last=4.105838e-03`; reinit-disabled comparator `_tmp_ch14_capillary_n32_t8_noreinit` blew up at `t=7.784`, confirming reinit remains needed for stability. Paper: formalized periodic quotient space, reinitializer closure/equivariance, true-zero-set-only Eikonal seed rule, wall-axis-only contact pinning, and periodic cyclic face-to-node reconstruction in `paper/sections/05_reinitialization.tex`, `03d_ridge_eikonal.tex`, `10d_ridge_eikonal_nonuniform.tex`, and `appendix_numerics_solver_s4.tex`. | session_CHK | CHK-RA-CH9-AFFINE-GAUGE-001 DONE 2026-04-30 — User 指示「affineの核心条件『既知ジャンプを満たす圧力なら cut-face flux が消える』が壊れる理由を理論的に裏付けして。それをもって、論文から削除したい」対応。Theory: affine cut-face flux is one coupled face operator `F_{\Gamma,f}=\alpha_f(G_f(p)-B_f(j_\Gamma))`; the known-jump zero-flux invariant requires the same nonzero cut-face coefficient to multiply both the pressure-gradient part and the jump lifting. A detached phase-block / per-phase Neumann gauge sets the cross-phase pressure coefficient to zero; if the known-jump coefficient remains nonzero, a pressure satisfying the jump still leaves residual cut-face flux, while setting it to zero removes the capillary drive itself. Therefore production affine has one global null mode and uses a fixed global gauge/pin, not phase-mean gauge. Paper: `paper/sections/09b_split_ppe.tex`, `paper/sections/09e_ppe_bc.tex`, `paper/sections/09f_pressure_summary.tex` updated to remove production endorsement of phase-mean gauge and document the invariant failure. Validation: `git diff --check` PASS; `latexmk -xelatex -interaction=nonstopmode -halt-on-error main.tex` PASS (`paper/main.pdf`, 234 pp). [SOLID-X] paper-only; no production code change. |

(ii) bare scalar `g` は §2 のベクトル `\bm{g}` 規約違反; (iii) 重力項に密度乗算 ρ が抜けて NS_onefluid と形式不一致 (物理的にも体積力は `ρ\bm{g}`)。L233 を「`+ [\mathcal{V}(\bm{u}) - \bnabla p + \sigma\kappa_{lg}\bnabla\psi + \rho\bm{g}]_i`」に修正 + 直後に inline 注記「ここで $\mathcal{V}(\bm{u}) = \bnabla\cdot[\mu(\bnabla\bm{u}+\bnabla\bm{u}^T)]$ は §\ref{sec:onefluid} と §\ref{sec:viscous_3layer} で定義された粘性演算子」を追加。これで §2 NS_onefluid → §6c FCCD closure → §7 viscous operator の 3 段で同一の symbol `\mathcal{V}(\bm{u})` と `ρ\bm{g}` が使われ、§6c closure を §2/§7 governing form に直接対応付けられる構造に統一。**(c12) Pass 1 + Pass 2 final ledger close-out — this commit**。**Validation**: 各 commit 後に `cd paper && latexmk -xelatex -interaction=nonstopmode -halt-on-error main.tex` PASS (234 pp 維持; | CHK-168 | 2026-04-21 | fix+test+wiki | [DONE] split-reinit y-flip 非対称 (binary-search B) root cause を特定 + 修正. ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# § LESSONS (KL-01 .. KL-12)

## §A — Known Error Classes (Math/Code)

| KL | Failure | Fix Pattern |
|---|---|---|
| KL-01 | Block matrix (2,1) sign flip after RHS transposition | Read RHS coeff → negate → write to LHS |
| KL-02 | Wrong block size (3×3 vs 2×2) in docs | Verify block dims against actual code arrays |
| KL-03 | Pseudocode comment names wrong algorithm | Cross-check comment vs accumulation pattern |
| KL-04 | D(κf) ≠ κD(f) for varying κ | Expand D(κf) = κD(f) + f·∇κ — never factor variable coefficients |
| KL-05 | Nyquist modified wavenumber ≠ finite-grid spectral radius | Compute spectral radius of actual discrete matrix |
| KL-06 | Pre-asymptotic O(h⁴) mistaken for asymptotic | Confirm slope stability over ≥3 grid doublings |
| KL-07 | "Conservative" CFL rounding wrong direction | Conservative means SMALLER dt — floor for dt, ceiling for Nsteps |
| KL-08 | Kronecker C-order vs Fortran-order confusion | State convention explicitly; verify with N=2 example |
| KL-09 | PPE LGMRES-primary/LU-fallback vs LU-primary confusion | LGMRES primary; spsolve auto-fallback on non-convergence (pre-2026-04-15) |
| KL-10 | Collocated corrector "exact CCD-div-free" claim | RC PPE leaves ‖∇_RC·u^{n+1}‖=0 but CCD sense residual O(h²) |
| KL-11 | Pin-node excl still targets (0,0) after move to center | Use `pin_dof = ravel_multi_index(tuple(n//2 for n in grid.N), grid.shape)` |
| KL-12 | `\texorpdfstring` missing in math heading → xelatex infinite loop | Wrap ALL numbered headings with `$...$` in texorpdfstring; pre-compile grep scan required |
